***иго.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иго.html>и́го</a> (19110)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьgo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yugóm</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иго.html>и́го</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ígo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иго.html>и́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иго.html>и́га</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иго.html>и́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> yoke; slavery, oppression</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> yoke</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ярмо.html>ярмо́</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jarmó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнуть.html>гнёт</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gnjot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">igrá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:игорный.html>иго́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">igórnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gambling, playing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:игорный.html>иго́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бизнес.html>би́знес</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>igórnyj</b> bíznɛs</i> ― <span class="e-translation">gambling business</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:игорный.html>иго́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>igórnyj</b> dom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">gambling house, gaming house</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>го́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

***игра.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a> (667)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">igra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьgra</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">igrá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игры́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>и́гры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игр</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>game
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>igrá</b> v mjač</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ball game</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>a sport which is played (<i>also</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:спортивный.html>спорти́вная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a>)</li>
<li><i>(action)</i>: play in the following senses:
<ol><li>Activity for amusement only, especially among the young.</li>
<li>Similar activity, in young animals, as they explore their environment and learn new skills.</li>
<li>(<i>ethology</i>) "Repeated, incompletely functional behavior differing from more serious versions ..., and initiated voluntarily when ... in a low-stress setting."</li>
<li>An individual's performance in a sport or game.</li></ol></li>
<li>acting, performance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a></b> актёра</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>igrá</b> aktjóra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">an actor’s performance</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>role-playing (<i>also</i> ролевая <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a>)</li>
<li>playing <i>(a musical instrument)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гитара.html>гита́ре</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>igrá</b> na gitáre</i> ― <span class="e-translation">playing the guitar</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***игральный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:игральный.html>игра́льный</a> (22624)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">igrátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to play</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́льный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-álʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:игральный.html>игра́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">igrálʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>playing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:игральный.html>игра́льные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">igrálʹnyje kárty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">playing cards</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:игральный.html>игра́льные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>ко́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>igrálʹnyje</b> kósti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dice</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***играть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a> (425)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьgrati</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">ȉgrati</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">hrát</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">igrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыграть.html>сыгра́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поиграть.html>поигра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to play</li>
<li>to act, to perform
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:соло.html>со́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>igrátʹ</b> sólo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to solo</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to gamble</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a storm</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of wine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sparkle</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Derived verbs formed from prefixes ending with a consonant use the root form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ыгра́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ygrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> so that the prefix consonant remains non-palatal. (Compare the hard sign that appears between consonant-ending prefixes and roots beginning with /j/.)
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:иго.html>и́г</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:рать.html>ра́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-игр-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> descriptor, identifier, handle</li></ol>

***идентифицировавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:идентифицировать.html>идентифици́ровавший</a> (20381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идентифицировать.html>идентифици́ровавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">idɛntificírovavšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идентифицировать.html>идентифици́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idɛntificírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
